Hi all, so I tried some advice to the algorithm, and it didnt work well. And then since that Zohaib told me to focus on the compression first, I think that maybe I should try the initial version of the algorithm, so I run some test after implementing some optimization that we talked about to this version. Here are all the files that I used. Maybe you can have a look. I store all results in the results.txt file. The results are not bad I guess. I think that if we add some optimization for the pattern in the codetable, it will improve, like there are many overlaps in the patterns it founds. So please take a look and give me some advice.
